@# / /
skabs gnyis pa'i mtha' dpyod rje btsun chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi gsung dri ma med pa zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
@## / /
rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid rtogs pa ni /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su /
sbyor ba dang /
mtha' dpyad pa gnyis las /
dang po ni /
rnam mkhyen gyi rjes su lam shes 'chad pa'i rgyu mtshan yod de /
theg pa gsum gyi lam rdzogs par sgom pa'i lam shes ma thob par rnam mkhyen mi 'thob pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis de ltar bshad pa'i phyir /
gnyis pa ni /
rnam bshad snying po rgyan las /
kha cig lam gsum bden stong du mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes lam shes kyi mtshan nyid du 'dod pa mi 'thad de /
nyan thos kyi lam shes pa'i lam shes kyis mi rtag sogs bcu drug mngon sum du ma rtogs par 'gyur la /
de ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i shes mthong gis bltas nas 'da' bar bya ba'i mngon rtogs theg pa chen po'i mthong lam gyi dus na skyed pa mi srid par thal ba dang /
nyan thos kyi rigs can rjes su gzung ba'i ched du lam gsum gyi dang po sgom pa ma yin par thal ba dang /
mi rtag sogs bcu drug mngon sum du rtogs pa nyid kyis spros bral mngon sum du rtogs pa yin na ni /
slob lam na bden gnyis ngo bo tha dad du 'dzin pa'i dri ma zad par spangs pa yod @## / /
par thal ba dang /
mnyam rjes ngo bo gcig tu yod par thal ba sogs so / /
gzhan yang /
lam shes la zhi mtha' 'gog pa'i snying rje chen po lam shes kyis bsdus pa mi 'thad par thal ba dang /
byang chub sems dpa'i rgyud kyi dmigs pa med pa'i snying rjes kyang stong nyid mngon sum du ma rtogs na /
lam shes la des khyab par 'dod pa ni mi rigs pa kho na 'o / /
zhes gsungs /
'di'i don ni / /
rong TIk pa na re /
lam gsum bden med du mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes de /
lam shes kyi mtshan nyid zer na /
byang sems 'phags pa'i rgyud kyi mi rtag sogs bcu drug mngon sum du rtogs pa'i mkhyen pa chos can /
mtshan nyid der thal /

theg chen 'phags pa'i mkhyen pa yin pa'i phyir /
'dod na /

'dod na /

'dod pa'i phyir /
gzhan yang /
slob pa'i rgyud la mnyam gzhag dang rjes thob kyi gzhi mthun yod par thal /
byang 'phags kyi rgyud kyi chos nyid la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i mnyam gzhag ye shes des chos nyid mngon sum du gzigs pa'i gzigs dor /
shes bya ji snyed pa mngon sum du rtogs pa'i phyir /
ma grub na /
der thal /
byang 'phags kyi rgyud kyi chos nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes de'i gzigs ngor kun rdzob bden pa yod pa'i phyir /
ma grub na song /
der thal /
byang 'phags kyi rgyud kyi mi rtag sogs bcu drug mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes de chos nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes yin pa'i phyir /
ma grub na song /
der thal /
lam gsum bden stong du mngon sum du rtogs pa'i ye shes yin pa'i phyir /
ma grub na song /

byang sems mthong lam pa'i rgyud kyi snying rje chen po chos can| mtshan nyid der thal /

de lam gsum bden par 'dzin pa'i bden 'dzin dang 'dzin stangs dngos su 'gal bar thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
rnam 'grel las /
byams sogs rmongs dang 'gal med phyir / /
zhes gsungs pa mi 'thad par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
kho na re /
byang sems mthong lam pa'i rgyud kyi snying rje chen po des lam gsum bden stong du mngon sum du rtogs par thal /
des stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i phyir te /
des stong nyid rtogs pa'i phyir /
des bden med rtogs pa'i phyir te /
des bden med la dmigs pa'i phyir /
der thal /
des dmigs pa med pa la dmigs pa'i phyir /
ma grub na /
de chos can /
der thal /
dmigs pa med pa la dmigs pa'i snying rje yin pa'i phyir /
zer na /
ma khyab /

de sems can bden stong gi rnam pa can gyi blo yang yin /
de sems can sdug bsngal dang bral 'dod kyi rnam pa can gyi blo yang yin pa'i phyir /

de chos can /
der thal /

ma khyab na /

Tikar /

zhes sogs kyi lung de'i don ni /

zhes gsungs /
rigs pas dpyad na /

de'i phyir /

der thal /

chos can de yin pa'i phyir /

bar chad med lam yin pa'i phyir /
gzhan yang /

rtags song /
'dod na /

de'i phyir /
der thal /
stong nyid kyi don spyi dngos yul du byed pa'i sems dpa'i rnal 'byor yin pa'i phyir te /
de stong nyid don spyi'i tshul gyis rtogs pa'i blo yin pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
mnyam gzhag ye shes yin na rjes thob ye shes yin dgos par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
gal te /

ma grub na /
der thal /
theg chen gyi mthong lam de la theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes dang theg chen gyi mthong lam rdzes thob ye shes gnyis su grangs nges pa ni gang zhig /
de theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes ma yin pa'i phyir /
dang po grub ste /
theg chen gyi mthong lam de la kun rdzob dngos yul du byed pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam dang /
don dam dngos yul du byed pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam gnyis su grangs nges pa'i phyir /
zer na /
ma khyab /
mthong lam sdug bsngal chos bzod la gnas pa'i sems dpa'i rgyud kyi gang zag gi bdag med mngon sum du rtogs pa'i mkhyen pa rjes thob ye shes su thal /
de'i rgyud la de yod pa gang zhig /

theg chen gyi mthong lam de la theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes dang rjes thob ye shes gnyis su grangs nges pa'i phyir /

der thal /

khyab ste /
zhi gnas yin na mnyam gzhag yin dgos pa'i phyir te /
phyi rol pa'i rgyud la mnyam gzhad yod pa'i phyir te /
de'i rgyud la mnyam gzhag gi sas bsdus kyi shes pa yod pa'i phyir te /

gong gi rtags ma grub na /

de'i rgyud la bsam gtan gyi dngos gzhi snyoms 'jug yod pa'i phyir zer /

de yod par thal /

dang po grub ste /

rang lugs la /
rang rgyud ldan gyi gang zag gi rgyud kyi stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis zin pa'i theg chen 'phags pa'i mngon par rtogs pa de lam shes kyi mtshan nyid /

mtha' dpyad pa gnyis /
dang po ni /
de bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis lam shes kyi mdo 'chad pa'i 'khor du lhags pa'i 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams kyi 'od mog mog por mdzad pa chos can /
dgos pa yod de /
lam shes kyi mdo 'chad pa'i 'khor du lhags pa'i 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams kyi rgyud la theg chen sems bskyed dang /
lam shes myur du skye ba'i snod rung du bsgrub pa'i ched yin pa'i phyir /
lam shes dngos su skye ba'i rten gyi yul so sor nges pa yin te /
lam shes dngos su skye ba'i rten gyi gang zag yin na /
byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gang zag yin dgos pa'i phyir /
byang chub sems dpa' las gzhan pa'i gang zag gi rgyud la lam shes skye mi rung ba ma yin te /
sems can thams @# / /
cad la sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyis khyab pa'i phyir /
dman lam sngon du ma song ba'i byang sems 'phags pa chos can /
khyod kyi rgyud kyi lam shes de nyan thos kyi lam las rang bzhin gyi khyad par du 'phags pa yin te /
khyod rang rgyud kyi 'dod pa'i zag pa dang /
srid pa'i zag pa rnams gzhan don byed pa'i yan lag tu sgyur bar byed pa'i rgyal sras 'phags pa yin pa'i phyir /
yang de chos can /
khyod kyi rgyud kyi lam shes de nyan thos kyi lam las byed las kyi sgo nas khyad par du 'phags pa yin te /
khyod kyi rgyud kyi lam shes des sems can mtha' yas pa smin grol la 'god par byed pa'i phyir /
gnyis pa la kha cig /
lam shes kyi rgyu ngo bo 'bras bu gsum po gang rung gis bsdus pa'i sems dpa'i yon tan de lam shes kyi yan lag gi mtshan nyid yin zer na /
rnam mkhyen chos can /
sems dpa'i yon tan yin par thal /
lam shes kyi yan lag yin pa'i phyir /
rtags grub ste /
sangs rgyas kyi sa na lam shes kyi yan lag yod pa'i phyir te /
de na yan lag can gyi lam shes yod pa'i phyir te /
de na lam shes yod pa'i phyir /
gzhan yang /
lam ma zhugs gang zag gi rgyud la lam shes kyi yan lag med par thal /
mtshan nyid de 'thad pa'i phyir /
'dod mi nus te /
theg pa chen por rigs sad pa de lam shes kyi yan lag yin pa'i phyir te /
yul nges pa dang /
khyab pa dang /
zhes pa'i gzhung gi don grub pa'i phyir /
kho na re /
lam shes kyi rang bzhin lam shes kyi yan lag yin par thal /
theg pa chen po'i rigs sad pa de lam shes kyi yan lag yin pa'i phyir /
rtags khas /
'dod na /
lam shes kyi ngo bo lam shes kyi yan lag yin par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod khyod kyi yan lag ma yin par thal /
bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
zer na /
lan 'og tu 'chad / /
! / /
rang lugs ni /
lam shes kyi rgyu ngo bo 'bras bu gsum po gang rung gis bsdus pa'i snying rje chen pos zin pa'i yon tan khyad par can de /
lam shes kyi yan lag gi mtshan nyid /
de la dbye na lnga yod do / /
sa mtshams theg pa chen po'i rigs sad pa nas /
sangs rgyas kyi sa'i bar na yod /
rtsod pa spong ba la kho na re /
lam shes chos can /
lam shes kyi yan lag yin par thal /
mtshan nyid de 'thad pa'i phyir /
ma grub na /
der thal /
lam shes yin pa'i phyir /
rtsa bar 'dod na /
lam shes chos can /
khyod khyod kyi yan lag ma yin par thal /
khyod bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
zhes bkag nas /
lam shes rdzogs byed kyi cha shas su gyur pa'i sems dpa'i yon tan de /
'dir bstan lam shes kyi yan lag gi mtshan nyid zer na /
nang 'gal te /
'dir bstan lam shes yin na /
lam shes rdzogs byed kyi cha shas su gyur pa'i sems dpa'i yon tan yin dgos par thal /
'dir bstan lam shes kyi yan lag yin na /
lam shes rdzogs byed kyi cha shas su gyur pa'i sems dpa'i yon tan yin dgos pa'i phyir /
rtags song /
'dod na /
skabs 'dir bstan gyi lam shes chos can /
der thal /
de'i phyir /
'dod na /
de chos can /
skabs 'dir bstan gyi lam shes kyi yan lag yin par thal /
lam shes rdzogs byed kyi cha shas su gyur pa'i sems dpa'i yon tan yin pa'i phyir /
rtags grub /
khyab pa song /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod khyod kyi yan lag ma yin par thal /
khyod bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
'khor gsum /
gzhan yang 'phags lam chos can /
khyod khyod kyi yan lag ma yin par thal /
khyod bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
khyab pa song /
'dod na /
'phags lam chos can /
khyod 'phags lam gyi yan lag yin par thal /
khyod 'phags lam yan lag yin pa'i phyir /
khyab ste /
byang chub yan lag yin na byang chub kyi yan lag yin dgos pa'i phyir /
rtags bud /
kha cig /
theg chen gyi sgom lam chos can /
khyod khyod kyi byed pa ma yin par thal /
khyod bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
khyab pa 'grig /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod theg chen gyi sgom lam gyi byed pa yin par thal /
khyod theg chen gyi sgom lam sgom stobs kyis thob pa'i phan yon yin pa'i phyir /
de bzhin du /
theg chen gyi sbyor ba chos can /
khyod khyod kyi yon tan ma yin par thal /
khyod bdag med yin pa'i phyir /
khyab pa khas blangs so / /
zhes zer / /
! / /
de yang byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa @# / /
kho na yin pas yul so sor nges pa yin no / /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su /
sbyor ba dang /
mtha' dpyad pa gnyis las /
dang po ni /
rtsa ba'i sbyor ba gnyis pa 'god /
gnyis pa la kha cig /
lam shes chos can /
khyod dngos su skye ba'i rten gyi yul so sor nges pa yin te /
byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gang zag kho na'i rgyud la dngos su skye ba'i phyir /
zer na /
sangs rgyas 'phags pa'i rgyud la rnam mkhyen dngos su skye bar thal /
rnam mkhyen rgyud ldan gyi gang zag yin na /
rang rgyud la rnam mkhyen dngos su mi skye bas ma khyab pa'i phyir /
ma grub na song /
der thal /
lam shes rgyud ldan yin na /
rang rgyud la lam shes dngos su mi skye bas ma khyab pa'i phyir /
ma grub na song /
byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gang zag chos can /
der thal /
de'i phyir /
ma grub na /
der thal /
khyod gang zag gang zhig /
lam shes khyod kyi rgyud la yod pa'i phyir /
ma grub na /
lam shes chos can /
byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gang zag gi rgyud la khyod yod par thal /
khyod byang 'phags kyi rgyud la yod pa'i phyir /
rtsa bar 'dod na /
sangs rgyas 'phags pa chos can /
khyod 'tshang rgya bar thal /
khyod kyi rgyud la rnam mkhyen dngos su skye ba'i phyir /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod 'tshang rgya 'gyur gyi gang zag yin par thal /
khyod gang zag gang zhig /
khyod 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir ro / /
! / /
rang lugs la /
lam shes dngos su gsar du skye ba'i rten gyi gang zag yin na /
byang chub sems dpa' yin pas khyab byas pa la /
kho na re /
lam shes de khams gsum gang rung gi rten la dngos su gsar du mi skye bar thal /
de 'dod pa'i gang zag gi rten la dngos su gsar du mi skye de gzugs khams pa dang /
gzugs med khams pa'i gang zag gi rten la yang dngos su gsar du mi skye ba'i phyir /
dang po ma grub na /
'dod pa'i rten can gyi gang zag de lam shes dngos su gsar du skye ba'i rten gyi gang zag yin par thal /
ma grub pa de'i phyir /
'dod na /
'dod pa'i gang zag chos can /
byang chub sems dpa' yin par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
rtags grub /
khyab pa khas /
zhes zer ro / /
! / /
theg pa gsum rnam par bzhag pa ni dgongs pa can yin gyi /
mtshan nyid pa ni ma yin no / /
zhes lugs las 'byung bas skye bo thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa can yin /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su /

mtha' dpyad pa gnyis las /
dang po ni /
khams gsum la 'dod chags dang bral ba'i nyan rang dgra bcom pa dang khams gsum la 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i rnal 'byor pa rnams chos can /
khyod la sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyis khyab pa yin te /
khyod sangs rgyas thob phyir du lam shes bsgom dgos kyi gang zag yin pa'i phyir /
de rnams kyi sangs rgyas thob phyir du lam shes bsgom dgos te /
sems can thams cad sangs rgyas pa'i dus srid pa'i phyir te /
mthar thug theg pa gcig tu grub pa'i phyir /
sems can thams cad sangs rgyas pa'i dus srid pa la mthar thug thag pa gsum du grub par ston pa'i lung gis mi gnod de /
mthar thug theg pa gsum du grub par ston pa'i mdo drang don dgongs pa can gyi mdo yin gyi /
nges don mtshan nyid pa ni ma yin no / /
zhes shing rta chen po klu sgrub dang thogs med gnyis kyi lugs las 'byung ba'i phyir /
kho na re /
tshur mthong lhas byin tshad mas ma dmigs pa'i sa phyogs chos can /

mthar thug theg pa gcig tu grub pa'i phyir /

'dod na /

khyod sems can thams cad kyi khongs su 'dus pa'i phyir /
zhes zer ba mi 'thad de /
shes bya chos can /

tshur mthong lhas byin yod pa gang zhig /
chos de ma yin pa dang phan tshun tha dad du gyur pa'i tshur mthong lhas byin sems can thams cad kyi khongs su ma 'dus pa'i phyir /

rnam mkhyen chos can /

de mngon sum du rtogs pa'i rnam mkhyen yin pa'i phyir /
rtags grub ste /
de mngon sum du rtogs pa'i rnam mkhyen yod pa'i phyir /

de 'dra'i shes pa yod pa gang zhig /

rong TIk pa na re /
mthong lam skye ba'i rten de la rang stobs kyis skye ba'i rten dang /

za ma tog bkod pa'i mdo las /
yul wA ra NA sir 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gis yi dwags mang po bden pa mthong ba la bkod par gsungs pa'i phyir dang /
lha'i bu blo gros rab gnas kyis zhus pa'i mdo las /
'dod pa dang gzugs kyi lha'i bu bye ba phrag brgyas chos rnams la chos kyi mig rngul med cing dri ma dang bral ba rnam par dag pa thob bo / /
zhes gsungs pa'i phyir /
zhes gsungs pa mi 'thad de /
gtan la dbab par bsdu ba las /

der thal /

phyi ma gnyis grub ste /

mdo gnyis kyi don rang lugs kyi skabs su 'chad do /
Ti ka'i rjes 'brang kha cig /
khams gong ma'i rten la mthong lam gsar du skye ba yod gsungs pa yang mi 'thad de /
rnam bshad snying po rgyan las /
sgra mi snyan pa dang za ma dang ma ning ma gtogs pa'i mi dang 'dod lha'i rten la skye yi khams gong ma'i rten la ni ma yin te /
khams gong ma la skyo ba shas chung ba'i phyir zhes dang /
lam rim las /

kho na re /
khams gong ma'i rten la theg chen gyi mthong lam gsar du skye ba yod par thal /
de'i rten la lam shes gsar du skye ba yod pa'i phyir /
der thal /
lam shes kyi mdo 'chad pa'i 'khor du lhags pa'i 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams lam shes dngos su gsar du skye ba'i snod rung du bya ba'i phyir du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams kyi 'od mog mog por mdzad pa'i phyir /
der thal /
lha rnams rung bar bya ba'i phyir /
zhes gsungs pa'i phyir na ma khyab ste /
lam shes kyi mdo 'chad pa'i 'khor du lhags pa'i 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams lam @# / /
shes rgyud nas skye ba'i snod rung du bya ba'i phyir du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams kyi 'od mog mog por mdzad pa lung de'i don yin pa'i phyir /
de ltar ma yin na lam shes kyi mdo 'chad pa'i 'khor du lhags pa'i 'dod gzugs gang rung gi lha yin na /
lam shes dngos su gsar du skye ba'i rten gyi gang zag yin dgos par thal lo / /
de rnams lam shes dngos su gsar du skye ba'i snod rung du bsgrub pa'i phyir du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rang bzhin gyi 'od kyis 'dod gzugs kyi lha rnams kyi 'od mog mog por mdzad pa'i phyir /

don dam dpyod byed kyi tshad ma yin na /
tha snyad dpyod byed kyi tshad ma yin dgos par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
theg chen gyi mthong lam bar chad med lam gyi yul du gyur pa'i chos nyid de ma yin dgag yin par thal /
theg chen gyi mthong lam bar chad med lam des chos nyid dngos su rtogs pa'i shugs la kho rang rtogs pa'i phyir /
rtags khas /
zhes /
stong mthun chen mo las shes so / /
thal 'gyur dang bo'i rtsa bar ma khyab ste /
rang gi 'dzin stangs kyi yul du gyur pa'i kun rdzob bden pa dngos su rtogs pa'i tshad ma zhig la tha snyad dpyod byed kyi tshad mar 'jog pa'i phyir /
gzhan yang /
theg chen gyi mthong lam chos bzod kyi kho rang rtogs par thal /

'dod na /
gser 'phreng las /

de la mkhas pa kha cig /
kun btus las /

de chos can /

brten pa theg chen gyi mthong lam bshad pa gnyis las /
dang po la /
lus rten dang /
sems rten gnyis las /
dang po ni /
gling gsum gyi mi dang 'dod lha'i rten la theg chen gyi mthong lam dngos su skye ba yod de /
de rnams kyi rten la theg chen gyi mthong lam dngos su skye ba'i mthun rkyen tshang zhing /
'gal rkyen dang bral ba yod pa'i phyir /
gnyis pa ni /
theg chen gyi mthong lam de bsam gtan gyi dngos gzhi'i sems la brten nas skye ba yod de /
de dngos su skye ba'i sems rten yod de dngos su skye ba'i sems rten du gyur pa'i gzugs med kyi snyoms 'jug kyang med /
bsam gtan gyi nyer bsdogs kyang med /
'dod sems kyang med pa'i phyir /
gnyis pa la mtshan nyid dbye ba /
skye tshul dang gsum las /
dang po ni /
rang rgyud ldan gyi gang zag gi rgyud kyi stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis zin pa'i theg chen gyi bden pa mngon rtogs de /
theg chen gyi mthong lam gyi mtshan nyid /
de la dbye na /

de gnyis gang rung ma yin pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam dang gsum las /
dang po ni /

dbye na /
theg chen gyi mthong lam bar chad med lam dang /
theg chen gyi mthong lam rnam grol lam /
de gnyis gang rung ma yin pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes dang gsum /
dang po ni /
chos nyid la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i theg chen gyi bden pa mngon rtogs gang zhig /
rang gi ngos skal gyi spang byar gyur pa'i bden 'dzin kun brtags kyi sa bon gyi dngos gnyen byed pa de /
theg chen gyi mthong lam bar chad med lam gyi mtshan nyid /
dbye na theg chen gyi mthong lam bzod pa brgyad yod /
rang dang mnyam gzhag thun gcig las skye ba'i theg chen gyi mthong lam bar chad med lam gyi ngos skal gyi spang bya spangs pa gang zhig /
chos nyid la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i theg chen gyi bden pa mngon rtogs su dmigs pa de /
theg chen gyi mthong lam rnam grol lam gyi mtshan nyid /
dbye na /
theg chen gyi mthong lam shes pa brgyad yod /
gsum pa ni /
chos nyid la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i mnyam gzhag ye shes las langs pa'i rjes thob kyi rjes su slar yang stong nyid la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes dang /
gang zag gi bdag med la rtse gcig tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam lta bu'o / /
theg chen gyi mthong lam rdzes thob ye shes kyi mtshan nyid ni /
theg chen gyi mthong lam mnyam gzhag ye shes las langs pa'i theg chen gyi bden pa mngon rtogs gang zhig rang rgyud ldan gyi gang zag gi rgyud la mngon 'gyur du 'byung ba de yin zhing /
de gnyis gang rung ma yin pa'i theg chen gyi mthong lam ni /
theg chen gyi mthong lam sdug bsngal chos bzod la gnas pa'i sems dpa'i rgyud kyi kun rdzob sems bskyed dang /
mthong lam rjes thob ye shes la gnas pa'i sems dpa'i rgyud kyi stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa'i mkhyen pa lta bu'o / /
gsum pa skye tshul ni /

ma grub na der thal /

sa brgyad pa'i rnam grol lam chos can /
khyod rang gi ngo skal gyi dri mas dag pa na /
khyod kyi yul de yang rang gi ngo skal gyi dri mas dag pa yin te /
khyod rang gi ngo skal gyi dri mas dag pa'i dag pa dang /

de gnyis ka de'i ngo skal gyi dri ma dang bral ba'i phyir te /
de gnyis ka gang zag gi bdag dang bral ba gang zhig /
gang zag gi bdag dang sa brgyad pa'i rnam grol lam gyi ngo skal gyi sgrib pa med mtshungs yin pa'i phyir te /

'dod na /
khyod rang thob byed kyi thabs su gyur pa'i theg chen gyi lam bden bsgom pa la brten nas thob par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
nyan thos dgra bcom pa'i rtogs pa sngon du song ba'i theg chen gyi sbyor lam chos mchog chen po la gnas pa'i sems dpa'i rgyud la byang sems kyi lam bden yod par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
des byang sems kyi lam bden thob par thal lo / /
'dod na /
des theg chen gyi mthong lam thob par thal lo / /
'dod na /
des theg chen gyi 'phags lam thob par thal lo / /
'dod mi nus te /
de theg chen so skye yin pa'i phyir /
byas pa la kho na re /
byang sems kyi rgyud kyi 'gog bden yin na /
byang sems kyi 'gog bden yin dgos par thal /
byang 'phags kyi rgyud kyi 'gog bden yin na /
byang sems kyi 'gog bden yin dgos pa'i phyir /
der thal /
byang 'phags kyi rgyud kyi lam bden yin na /
byang sems kyi lam bden yin dgos pa'i phyir /
zer na ma khyab / / / /
sa dgu la ni chen po yis / /
zhes sogs kyi skabs su sbyor ba dang /
mtha' dpyad pa gnyis /
dang po ni /
sangs rgyas kyi rnam dag de @# / /
rnam dag shin tu ba yin pa dang /
nyan rang gi rnam dag rnam dag shin tu ba ma yin pa'i khyad par 'thad pa yin te /
theg chen gyi sgom lam bar chad med lam chung ngu'i chung ngu sogs dgus rang gi ngo skal gyi sgrib pa gnyis ka'i dngos gnyen byed nus /
nyan thos kyi sgom lam bar chad med lam chung ngu'i chung ngu sogs dgus rang gi ngo skal gyi sgrib pa gnyis kyi dngos gnyen byed mi nus pa'i phyir /
gnyis pa la kha cig /
theg chen gyi sgom lam bar chad med lam chung ngu'i chung ngu dang sa gnyis pa'i sgom lam bar chad med lam don gcig pa nas bzung ste /
theg chen gyi sgom lam chen po'i chen po dang /
sa bcu pa'i sgom lam don gcig zer na /
sa dang po'i sgom lam bar chad med lam chos can /
sa gnyis pa'i sgom lam yin par thal /
theg chen gyi sgom lam bar chad med lam chung ngu'i chung ngu yin pa'i phyir /
khyab pa khas /
ma grub na /
der thal /
de yod pa'i phyir /
der thal /
sa dang po'i sgom lam yod pa gang zhig /
theg chen gyi sgom lam thob na /
theg chen gyi sgom lam bar chad med lam thob pas khyab pa'i phyir /
phyi ma bud /
dang po ma grub na /
der thal /
sa bcu pa'i sgom lam yod pa'i phyir /
der thal /
kun btus las /
byang chub sems dpa'i rnams ni sa bcu rnams su sgom lam la shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po'i lam bsgom kyis nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnyen po ma yin no / /
zhes pa dang /
'grel chen las /
de bas na /
sa dang po'i skad cig ma dang po ni mthong ba'i lam yin la /
de las gzhan ba skad cig gnyis pa la sogs pa ni rdo rje lta bur brjod pa'i bar chad med pa'i lam gang las de ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi sa kun tu 'od thob pa'i bar 'di dag thams cad ni chos kyi dbyings mchog gi don la sogs pa so sor rtogs pa'i phyir sgom pa'i lam yin par brjod do / /
zhes gsungs pa'i phyir /
rtsa bar 'dod na sla /
kho na re /
sa dang po'i sgom lam bar chad med lam chos can /
khyod bden 'dzin chen po'i chen po'i dngos gnyen bar chad med lam yin par thal /
theg chen gyi sgom lam bar chad med lam chung ngu'i chung ngu yin pa'i phyir /
rtags sla /
'dod na /
sa gnyis pa'i sgom lam bar chad med lam des /
bden 'dzin chen po'i chen po spangs par thal /
'dod pa'i phyir /
'dod na /
de ma spangs par thal /
de'i ngo skal gyi spang byar gyur pa'i bden 'dzin chen po'i chen po gcig yod pa'i phyir /
rtags sla /
zer na rtsa bar ma khyab ste /
sa bcu pa'i rnam grol lam des bden 'dzin chung ngu'i chung ngu spangs par thal| de theg chen gyi sgom lam rnam grol lam chen po'i chen po yin pa'i phyir /
khyab pa khas /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod kyis bden 'dzin spangs par thal /
khyod kyis bden 'dzin chung ngu'i chung ngu spangs pa'i phyir /
rtags khas /
'dod na /
de chos can /
khyod sangs rgyas yin par thal /
khyod kyis bden 'dzin spangs pa'i phyir /
skabs gnyis pa'i mtha' dpyod rje btsun chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi gsung dri ma med pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so / / / /
sher phyin man ngag snying po'i dka' ba'i gnad / /
lung rig lam nas drangs te ma nor bar / /
gsal mdzad chos kyi rgyal mtshan de'i bzhed srol / /
brgyud 'dzin dang bcas bskal brgyar dar rgyas shog / / /

rnam grol zhi ba'i rgya mtshor ro gcig tu / /
gzhol ba'i mtha' yas chos tshul dal 'babs klung / /
tshig gi gzegs ma res kyang dug gsum  @# / /
gyi| |dri ma yongs 'khrud legs bshad bdud rtsi 'di / /
dpar du bskrun pa'i rnam dkar phung po'i mthus / /
yang dag chos kyi sgo mo stong phrag brgya / /
gdangs te rgyud lnga'i 'gro ba ma lus pa / /
des legs nor bu'i mdzod la dbang 'byor shog / / /
ces pa 'di yang ser byes lho dge bshes blo bzang dang / /
rgyud smad sngags ram ba tshwa ba ngag dbang nor bu /
